msg:Every time I come to Hefei, I will stay at Huifeng Wanyun Hotel. The hotel is comparable to a five-star hotel (although I don't know the exact number of stars), but the hotel lobby is very grand, the rooms are also very upscale, and the floors are very high with a very good view. You can overlook Chaohu Lake. The hotel parking lot is very large and parking is convenient. During the May Day holiday, the business was very good and the hotel was basically fully booked, which shows that it is indeed popular. The key is that the price is affordable and it is worth staying.

There is no self-service laundry room, which is also a headache. Although many star-rated hotels do not have it. . .
